"\nText\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n|\n\n\n\n52014PC0166\n\nProposal for a REGULATION OF THE EUROPEAN PARLIAMENT AND OF THE COUNCIL on the reduction or elimination of customs duties on goods originating in Ukraine /* COM/2014/0166 final - 2014/0090 (COD) */\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nEXPLANATORY MEMORANDUM\n1.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 CONTEXT OF THE PROPOSAL\nOn 21 November 2013, Ukraine announced the suspension of the preparations for the\nsignature of the Association Agreement, including a Deep and Comprehensive Free\nTrade Area (DCFTA) with the EU. \nFollowing the recent unprecedented\nevents in the country and the security, political and economic challenges faced\nby Ukraine, on 6 March 2014, the\nEuropean Council stated its intention to support the economic stabilization of\nthe country by means of a package of measures, including the granting of autonomous trade preferences. \nThis measure will allow for the Union's\nunilateral reduction or elimination of customs duties on goods originating in\nUkraine, in accordance with the Schedule of concessions set out in Annex I-A to\nthe Association Agreement between the EU and Ukraine. \n2.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 RESULTS OF CONSULTATIONS\nWITH INTERESTED PARTIES AND IMPACT ASSESSMENT\nNot applicable. \n3.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 LEGAL ELEMENTS OF THE\nPROPOSAL\nThe legal basis for the proposal is\nArticle 207(2) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union.\n4.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 BUDGETARY IMPLICATION \nThe European Union will see a loss of\ncustoms revenue corresponding to EUR 487 million (gross) annually. However,\nthose figures are estimates, having regard to the economic situation of Ukraine and can change.\n2014/0090 (COD)\nProposal for a\nREGULATION OF THE EUROPEAN PARLIAMENT\nAND OF THE COUNCIL\non the reduction or elimination of customs\nduties on goods originating in Ukraine\nTHE EUROPEAN PARLIAMENT AND THE\nCOUNCIL OF THE EUROPEAN UNION,\nHaving regard to the Treaty on the\nFunctioning of the European Union, and in particular Article 207(2) thereof,\nHaving regard to the proposal from the\nEuropean Commission,\nAfter transmission of the draft legislative\nact to the national Parliaments,\nActing in accordance with the ordinary\nlegislative procedure,\nWhereas:\n(1)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Ukraine is a priority partner country within the\nEuropean Neighbourhood Policy (ENP) and the Eastern Partnership. The European Union\nhas been seeking an increasingly close relationship with Ukraine going beyond mere bilateral cooperation, encompassing gradual progress towards\npolitical association and economic integration. In this respect, the European\nUnion and Ukraine negotiated in 2007-2011 an Association\nAgreement, including a Deep and Comprehensive Free Trade Area (DCFTA), which\nwas initialed by both parties in 2012. Under the provisions of the DCFTA, the\nEuropean Union and Ukraine are to establish a free trade area over a\ntransitional period of a maximum of 10 years starting from the entry into force\nof the Association Agreement, in accordance with Article XXIV of the General\nAgreement on Tariffs and Trade 1994.\n(2)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 In light of the unprecedented security, political and economic challenges\nfaced by Ukraine, and in order to support its economy, it\nis appropriate not to await the entry into force of the Association Agreement's\nprovisions on a Deep and Comprehensive Free Trade Area (DCFTA), but to anticipate\nits implementation by means of autonomous trade preferences and to start unilaterally\nthe reduction or elimination of Union customs duties on goods originating in\nUkraine, in accordance with the Schedule of concessions set out in Annex I-A to\nthe Association Agreement. \n(3)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 In\norder to prevent any risk of fraud, the entitlement to benefit from autonomous\ntrade preferences should be conditional on the compliance by Ukraine with the relevant rules of origin of products and the procedures related thereto as well as\ninvolvement in effective administrative cooperation with the Union. Moreover, Ukraine should abstain from introducing new duties or charges having equivalent effect or\nnew quantitative restrictions or measures having equivalent effect or from\nincreasing existing levels of duties or charges or from introducing any other\nrestrictions. In the event of failure to comply with any of these conditions\nthe Commission should be empowered to suspend temporarily all or part of the\npreferences.\n(4)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 It is\nnecessary to provide for the reintroduction of normal Common Customs Tariff\nduties for any products which cause, or threaten to cause, serious difficulties\nto Union producers of like or directly competing products, subject to an\ninvestigation by the Commission.\n(5)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 The\nmeasures necessary for the implementation of this Regulation should be adopted\nin accordance with Regulation (EU)\nNo 182/2011 of the European Parliament and of the Council.[1]\n(6)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 In view of the urgency of\nthe matter, it is important to apply an exception to the eight-week period\nreferred to in Article 4 of Protocol No 1 on the role of national Parliaments\nin the European Union, annexed to the Treaty on European Union and to the\nTreaty on the Functioning of the European Union,\nHAVE ADOPTED THIS REGULATION:\nArticle 1\nPreferential\narrangements\nCustoms duties on goods originating in Ukraine shall be reduced or eliminated in accordance with Annex I to this Regulation.\nArticle 2\nConditions\nfor entitlement to the\npreferential arrangements\nEntitlement to benefit from the preferential arrangements introduced by Article 1 shall be subject\nto:\n(a)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 compliance with the rules of origin\nof products and the procedures related thereto as provided for in Title IV,\nChapter 2, section 2 of Regulation (EEC) No 2454/93[2];\n(b)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 compliance with the methods of\nadministrative cooperation as provided for in Articles 121 and 122 of\nRegulation (EEC) No 2454/93;\n(c)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 participation by Ukraine in effective administrative cooperation with the Union in order to prevent any risk of\nfraud;\n(d)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 abstention by Ukraine from\nintroducing new duties or charges having equivalent effect and new quantitative\nrestrictions or measures having equivalent effect for imports originating in\nthe Union or from increasing existing levels of duties or charges or from\nintroducing any other restrictions from the day of the entry into force of this\nRegulation.\nArticle 3\nAccess\nto tariff quotas\n1.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Products listed in Annexes II\nand III shall be admitted for import into the Union within the limits of Union\ntariff quotas as set out in those Annexes.\n2.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 The tariff quotas referred to\nin paragraph 1 shall be administered by the Commission in accordance with\nArticles 308a, 308b and 308c of Regulation (EEC) No 2454/93, with the exception\nof the tariff quotas for specific agricultural products referred to in Annex\nIII.\n3.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Tariff quotas for specific agricultural\nproducts referred to in Annex III shall be administered by the Commission\npursuant to the rules laid down in accordance with Article 184 of Regulation\n(EU) No 1308/2013[3].\nArticle 4\nTemporary\nsuspension\nWhere the Commission finds that there is\nsufficient evidence of failure to comply with the conditions set out in Article 2 it may suspend in whole or in\npart the preferential arrangements provided for in this Regulation, in\naccordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article 6(2).\nArticle 5\nSafeguard\nclause\nWhere imports of a product originating in\nUkraine and included in Annex I cause or threaten to cause serious difficulties\nto Union producers of like or directly competing products the Commission may\nreintroduce the normal Common Customs Tariff duties with regard to such imports\nsubject to the conditions and in accordance with the procedures laid down in Articles 11 and 11a of Council Regulation\n(EC) No 55/2008[4]\nwhich shall apply mutatis mutandis.\nArticle 6\nCommittee\nprocedure\n1.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 For the implementation of\nArticle 3(2) and Article 4 of this Regulation, the Commission shall be assisted\nby the Customs Code Committee instituted by Article 248a of Regulation (EEC) No 2913/92. The Committee shall be a committee within\nthe meaning of Regulation (EU) No 182/2011. \n2.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Where reference is made to this paragraph, Article 5 of\nRegulation (EU) No 182/2011 shall apply.\nArticle 7\nEntry\ninto force and\napplication\nThis Regulation shall enter into force on\nthe day following that of its publication in the Official Journal of the\nEuropean Union.\nIt shall apply until the Association Agreement between the European Union and its Member States, of the one part, and Ukraine, of the other part, enters into force or, where\nappropriate, is applied provisionally. \nIt shall cease to apply on 1 November 2014.\nThe Commission shall publish in the Official Journal of the European\nUnion a notice in the event that this Regulation ceases to apply before 1\nNovember 2014.\nDone at Strasbourg,\nFor the European Parliament\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 For\nthe Council\nThe President\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 The\nPresident\n[1]\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Regulation (EU) No 182/2011 of the European\nParliament and of the Council of 16 February 2011 laying down the rules and\ngeneral principles concerning mechanisms for control by Member States of the\nCommission\u2019s exercise of implementing powers (OJ L 55, 28.2.2011, p. 13).\n[2]\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Commission\nRegulation (EEC) No 2454/93 of 2 July 1993 laying down provisions for the\nimplementation of Council Regulation (EEC) No 2913/92 establishing the\nCommunity Customs Code (OJ L 253, 11.10.1993, p. 1).\n[3]\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Council\nRegulations (EEC) No 922/72, (EEC) No 234/79, (EC) No 1037/2001 and (EC) No\n1234/2007 (OJ L 347, 20.12.2013, p. 671) Republic of Moldova and amending Regulation (EC) No\n980/2005 and Commission Decision 2005/924/EC (OJ L 20, 24.1.2008, p. 1). \nANNEX I\nTariff\nschedules of EU\n CN 2008 || DESCRIPTION || Base rate
